00:53:35","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 00:53:35","title":"Amazon adds device dashboard in bid to make Fire tablets a smart home control center","link":"https://techcrunch.com/?p=2066221","description":"<p class=\"p1\">It’s been a busy few weeks for the smart home race. <a class=\"crunchbase-link\" href=\"https://crunchbase.com/organization/amazon\" target=\"_blank\" data-type=\"organization\" data-entity=\"amazon\">Amazon, <span class=\"crunchbase-tooltip-indicator\"></span></a> Google and Apple have all announced new smart speakers aimed at — among other things — cementing their respective positions at the center of users’ connected households.</p>\n<p class=\"p1\">Adding onto the introduction of a whole bunch of new <a class=\"crunchbase-link\" href=\"https://crunchbase.com/organization/echo\" target=\"_blank\" data-type=\"organization\" data-entity=\"echo\">Echo <span class=\"crunchbase-tooltip-indicator\"></span></a> devices, Amazon is also improving what its famously inexpensive Fire Tablets can do. Today the company will be rolling out a free software update to select slates that brings a smart home device dashboard. The system essentially serves as a one-stop shop for connected devices that work with Alexa.</p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"qt3lixTD4d\"><p id=\"speakable-summary\"><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2020/10/22/amazon-echo-review-well-rounded-sound/\">Amazon Echo review: Well-rounded sound</a></p></blockquote><div class=\"piano-inline-promo\"></div>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts\" security=\"restricted\" title=\"&#8220;Amazon Echo review: Well-rounded sound&#8221; &#8212; TechCrunch\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/2020/10/22/amazon-echo-review-well-rounded-sound/embed/#?secret=qt3lixTD4d\" data-secret=\"qt3lixTD4d\" width=\"800\" height=\"450\" frameborder=\"0\" marginwidth=\"0\" marginheight=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"></iframe></div>\n<p class=\"p1\">It’s similar to the sorts of control centers Google and Apple offer with their respective Home apps, with access to things like smart lights, plugs, cameras, thermostats, you name it. Similar functionality can also be found on the Echo Show devices. Fire tablets offer a pretty cheap way in to that functionality (so, too, might Fire TVs, going forward). And, of course, Amazon has also made efforts to improve Alexa functionality on the devices, essentially letting them double as inexpensive smart displays.</p>\n<p>Perhaps the biggest piece of the puzzle, however, is the addition of smart home hub functionality on the new Echo. The fact was a bit under reported (Amazon, after all, started adding this functionality with previous Echo Plus models), but adding zigbee functionality for the $99 device should go a ways toward lowering that barrier of entry.</p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"2DuR6v3rWQ\"><p><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2020/09/24/this-is-the-newer-rounder-100-amazon-echo/\">This is the newer, rounder $100 Amazon Echo</a></p></blockquote>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" id=\"speakable-summary\"><a href=\"https://www.animaapp.com\">Anima</a>, the company that turns design prototypes into code, has today announced the launch of Anima 4.0, which will allow designers to create prototypes in Figma that are translated into components in React with the click of a button.</p>\n<p>The company was founded by <a class=\"crunchbase-link\" href=\"https://crunchbase.com/person/arbel-arbel\" target=\"_blank\" data-type=\"person\" data-entity=\"arbel-arbel\">Or Arbel <span class=\"crunchbase-tooltip-indicator\"></span></a> (cofounder of Yo!), Avishay Cohen (who led R&#38;D at Mobli) and Michal Cohen. It launched three years ago with a platform that allowed designers in Figma, Sketch and Adobe XD to translate their designs into HTML code. With today&#8217;s launch, those designs (in <a class=\"crunchbase-link\" href=\"https://crunchbase.com/organization/figma\" target=\"_blank\" data-type=\"organization\" data-entity=\"figma\">Figma <span class=\"crunchbase-tooltip-indicator\"></span></a> only, for the moment) can be turned into React components, giving developers the ability to tweak and polish individual components in a coding language that they&#8217;re already using.</p>\n<p>Enterprise design tools have absolutely blown up over the past several years. As opposed to a time where designers really only had the option to work in Photoshop and developers then had to spend time turning those static images into code, it&#8217;s fair to call the design landscape of 2020 crowded.</p><div class=\"piano-inline-promo\"></div>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"E7W4aD95d3\"><p><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2019/12/05/design-may-be-the-next-entrepreneurial-gold-rush/\">Design may be the next entrepreneurial gold rush</a></p></blockquote>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts\" security=\"restricted\" title=\"&#8220;Design may be the next entrepreneurial gold rush&#8221; &#8212; TechCrunch\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/2019/12/05/design-may-be-the-next-entrepreneurial-gold-rush/embed/#?secret=E7W4aD95d3\" data-secret=\"E7W4aD95d3\" width=\"800\" height=\"450\" frameborder=\"0\" marginwidth=\"0\" marginheight=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"></iframe></div>\n<p>Platforms like Sketch, InVision, and Figma have aimed to close the gap between designers and developers, and in the lattermost case, designers and other designers, as well. Adobe has also answered the call of growing competition with the launch of Adobe XD.</p>\n<p>Anima 4.0 represents yet another shift. The company is riding the wave of enterprise design tool growth, while simultaneously positioning itself in the realm of no-code, another high-growth vertical.</p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"rMoOXpE1zx\"><p><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2020/07/21/tracking-the-growth-of-low-code-no-code-startups/\">Tracking the growth of low-code, no-code startups</a></p></blockquote>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts\" security=\"restricted\" title=\"&#8220;Tracking the growth of low-code, no-code startups&#8221; &#8212; TechCrunch\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/2020/07/21/tracking-the-growth-of-low-code-no-code-startups/embed/#?secret=rMoOXpE1zx\" data-secret=\"rMoOXpE1zx\" width=\"800\" height=\"450\" frameborder=\"0\" marginwidth=\"0\" marginheight=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"></iframe></div>\n<p>Arbel told TechCrunch that, around the time that <a class=\"crunchbase-link\" href=\"https://crunchbase.com/organization/yo\" target=\"_blank\" data-type=\"organization\" data-entity=\"yo\">Yo <span class=\"crunchbase-tooltip-indicator\"></span></a> was shuttering, he knew that his next venture would be a product that charges money from day one. He also said that he and his cofounders had been frustrated for a long time by the disconnect between designers and developers.</p>\n<p>Thus, Anima was born. It costs $40/month to use Anima, or approximately $370 annually. Arbel confirmed to TechCrunch that pricing wouldn&#8217;t change with the launch of Anima 4.0 but that it may in the future. The reason for that is that Anima originally took developers out of the picture, allowing designers to build out their designs and translate it automatically into running HTML code.</p>\n<p>With this launch, Anima is looking to bring developers back into the fold, speaking to them in React (their native tongue, if you will). That opens the door to charging more per seat or introducing new revenue streams.</p>\n<p>Arbel said that Anima was profitable before it ever received its first funding, which came in the form of a $120K check from Y Combinator in the summer of 2018. This year, the company raised $2.5 million in seed funding led by Hetz Ventures, Zohar Gilon, and Ed Lando.</p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"awDaYwazJG\"><p><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2015/02/24/notifications-without-apps/\">Yo Tries To Make Itself Useful With Photo And Link Alerts From 150 Sources</a></p></blockquote>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts\" security=\"restricted\" title=\"&#8220;Yo Tries To Make Itself Useful With Photo And Link Alerts From 150 Sources&#8221; &#8212; TechCrunch\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/2015/02/24/notifications-without-apps/embed/#?secret=awDaYwazJG\" data-secret=\"awDaYwazJG\" width=\"800\" height=\"450\" frameborder=\"0\" marginwidth=\"0\" marginheight=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"></iframe></div>\n<p>Today, Anima is used by 300,000 designers, developers and product managers from companies like Google, Amazon,  Starbucks, and Walmart, among others. Each week, the Anima community converts more than 4,000 designs into code.</p>\n<p>The Anima team has grown from four at the onset of the pandemic to 17 now, with a 70/30 split between men and women.</p>\n<p>&#8220;The greatest challenge is making developer-friendly code,&#8221; said Arbel. &#8220;Developers are not an easy audience &#8212; I know because I&#8217;m a developer myself. We&#8217;ve been hearing about code generation and. the like since the beginning of the internet, and endless amounts of products have tried and none of them have managed to produce developer-friendly code. They product huge amounts of code that is bloated and hard to understand. href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2019/11/06/as-developers-embrace-kubernetes-replicated-launches-tools-to-manage-its-deployments/\"> the company shifted to service those applications</a>.</p><div class=\"piano-inline-promo\"></div>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"QrWZdsAgjk\"><p id=\"speakable-summary\"><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2019/11/06/as-developers-embrace-kubernetes-replicated-launches-tools-to-manage-its-deployments/\">As developers embrace Kubernetes, Replicated launches tools to manage its deployments</a></p></blockquote>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts\" security=\"restricted\" title=\"&#8220;As developers embrace Kubernetes, Replicated launches tools to manage its deployments&#8221; &#8212; TechCrunch\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/2019/11/06/as-developers-embrace-kubernetes-replicated-launches-tools-to-manage-its-deployments/embed/#?secret=QrWZdsAgjk\" data-secret=\"QrWZdsAgjk\" width=\"800\" height=\"450\" frameborder=\"0\" marginwidth=\"0\" marginheight=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"></iframe></div>\n<p>Last year, the company unveiled its tools for managing Kubernetes deployments and immediately saw sales increase.</p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">&#8220;That new offering changed the direction of the company and added velocity and customers and the market responded so well to it,&#8221; said Replicated chief executive, Grant Miller. &#8220;Once we started building on that success.. We brought on UIPath, Puppet, who created the software automation stuff, TripWire, and then these cool emerging software companies like FlatFile and Fishtown Analytics.&#8221;</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Replicated now counts 85 customers who pay for access to the platform and for every on-premise deployment that customers develop through the platform. &#8220;If you are a company like Puppet, you have hundreds of on-premise customers.&#8221;</span></p>\n<p>The company has already been staffing up with key c-suite hires including a chief product officer, a chief revenue officer and vice presidents of marketing and sales. Some of the money will support Replicated&#8217;s continued hiring push, while another chunk will go into product development.</p>\n<p dir=\"ltr\">&#8220;We&#8217;re automating as much of the manual software processes that require IT admins to put their hands on keyboards to adjust and optimize things,&#8221; said Miller. &#8220;With Replicated, half of the services are for tooling for the software vendor to manage release and licensing and the other half is for the IT admin. It&#8217;s about how they automate the integration of the applications.&#8221;<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> </span></p>\n<p>The company, which currently has 28 employees expects to grow to 75 staff members by the end of 2021, Miller said.</p>\n<p dir=\"ltr\">“The on-prem software market is four times larger than the SaaS market,” Miller said in a statement. “Replicated lets software vendors unlock the opportunity of the on-prem software category with lower engineering overhead and faster time to market. This is a market change made possible by the convergence of cloud native computing and Kubernetes.”</p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a 00:53:35","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 00:53:35","title":"Facetune maker’s new app Filtertune let anyone create and share personalized photo filters","link":"https://techcrunch.com/?p=2066213","description":"<p id=\"speakable-summary\"><a class=\"crunchbase-link\" href=\"https://crunchbase.com/organization/facetune\" target=\"_blank\" data-type=\"organization\" data-entity=\"facetune\">Facetune <span class=\"crunchbase-tooltip-indicator\"></span></a> maker <a href=\"https://www.lightricks.com/\">Lightricks</a> is out today with a new app, <a href=\"https://apps.apple.com/app/filtertune-filters-presets/id1511547935\">Filtertune</a>, designed to create a community around custom photo filters. With the app, creators can make their own personalized preset photos filters, then share them across social media as photos that have a special QR code attached. When others see a filter they like, they can screenshot it to import it back into the Filtertune app for their own use.</p>\n<p>While it would be easier to create some sort of in-app system for sharing filters &#8212; similar to Instagram&#8217;s &#8220;Effect Gallery,&#8221; for example &#8212; <a class=\"crunchbase-link\" href=\"https://crunchbase.com/organization/lightricks\" target=\"_blank\" data-type=\"organization\" data-entity=\"lightricks\">Lightricks&#8217; <span class=\"crunchbase-tooltip-indicator\"></span></a> user base isn&#8217;t concentrated in one single app.</p>\n<p>Instead, it offers an ever-expanding suite of mobile photo and video editing apps, including its flagship Facetune and sequel, Facetune2, as well as Facetune Video, Enlight Quickshot, Photofox, Videoleap, Pixaloop, Boosted, Seen, PosterBoost, Artleap, and Beatleap.</p><div class=\"piano-inline-promo\"></div>\n<p><div id=\"attachment_2066303\" style=\"width: 690px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-2066303\" loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-2066303\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/App-Store-Screens.jpg?w=680\" alt=\"\" width=\"680\" height=\"201\" srcset=\"https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/App-Store-Screens.jpg 5001w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/App-Store-Screens.jpg?resize=150,44 150w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/App-Store-Screens.jpg?resize=300,89 300w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/App-Store-Screens.jpg?resize=768,227 768w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/App-Store-Screens.jpg?resize=680,201 680w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/App-Store-Screens.jpg?resize=1536,455 1536w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/App-Store-Screens.jpg?resize=2048,606 2048w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/App-Store-Screens.jpg?resize=50,15 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 680px) 100vw, 680px\" /><p id=\"caption-attachment-2066303\" class=\"wp-caption-text\"><strong>Image Credits:</strong> Lightricks</p></div></p>\n<p>Combined, its collection of apps have seen over 400 million downloads to date, but its active user numbers are much smaller. Lightricks <a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2020/07/28/facetune-maker-lightricks-brings-its-popular-selfie-retouching-features-to-video/\">this summer said</a> its collection of apps had 200 million registered users. Paid subscribers had reached 3 million <a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2019/10/02/facetune-maker-lightricks-expands-with-a-trio-of-apps-for-small-businesses/\">as of last year</a>.</p>\n<p>While these numbers and the apps&#8217; growth helped <a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2019/07/31/the-maker-of-popular-selfie-app-facetune-just-landed-135-million-at-a-unicorn-valuation/\">to turn Lightricks into a unicorn</a>, Instagram offers access to a much larger photo sharing community. That&#8217;s why it makes sense for Filtertune to provide tools that allow users to tap into existing social media platforms to share their filters and discover new ones.</p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"JzS6BJjum7\"><p><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2019/07/31/the-maker-of-popular-selfie-app-facetune-just-landed-135-million-at-a-unicorn-valuation/\">The maker of popular selfie app Facetune just landed $135 million at a unicorn valuation</a></p></blockquote>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts\" security=\"restricted\" title=\"&#8220;The maker of popular selfie app Facetune just landed $135 million at a unicorn valuation&#8221; &#8212; TechCrunch\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/2019/07/31/the-maker-of-popular-selfie-app-facetune-just-landed-135-million-at-a-unicorn-valuation/embed/#?secret=JzS6BJjum7\" data-secret=\"JzS6BJjum7\" width=\"800\" height=\"450\" frameborder=\"0\" marginwidth=\"0\" marginheight=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"></iframe></div>\n<p>In fact, Lightricks says the idea for the app was actually prompted by social media trends where online influencers were posting &#8220;How I Edit My Photos,&#8221; and offering their own presets for fans to download or purchase.</p>\n<p>Filtertune, however, isn&#8217;t a marketplace for filters. It&#8217;s just a tool for creation, editing and sharing.</p>\n<p>Using the app, you can either edit an existing filter or create one of your own from scratch.</p>\n<p>The app focuses on realistic photo editing, not using overlays of digital assets to create new styles &#8212; like apps that swap out the background, for example, or those that use AR.</p>\n<p>When your filter is complete, you tap the sharing button which adds a banner to your photo that reads: &#8220;Get this filter,&#8221; and offers download instructions along with a QR code. You then save this image to your iPhone Camera Roll, then post it anywhere you want &#8212; like Facebook, Instagram, Twitter, Snapchat, in an email, in a messaging app, or on your own website.</p>\n<p>When others see the shared image, they save it to their own Camera Roll by taking a screenshot.</p>\n<p>The next time those users open the Filtertune app, it will scan for new filters by looking for images with a QR code. When it finds them, the new filters will be added to the in-app collection.</p>\n<p><div id=\"attachment_2066302\" style=\"width: 690px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-2066302\" loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-2066302\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Filtertune-Results-With-Filter-Tag.png?w=680\" alt=\"\" width=\"680\" height=\"678\" srcset=\"https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Filtertune-Results-With-Filter-Tag.png 1284w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Filtertune-Results-With-Filter-Tag.png?resize=150,150 150w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Filtertune-Results-With-Filter-Tag.png?resize=300,300 300w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Filtertune-Results-With-Filter-Tag.png?resize=768,766 768w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Filtertune-Results-With-Filter-Tag.png?resize=680,678 680w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Filtertune-Results-With-Filter-Tag.png?resize=32,32 32w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Filtertune-Results-With-Filter-Tag.png?resize=50,50 50w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Filtertune-Results-With-Filter-Tag.png?resize=64,64 64w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Filtertune-Results-With-Filter-Tag.png?resize=96,96 96w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Filtertune-Results-With-Filter-Tag.png?resize=128,128 128w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 680px) 100vw, 680px\" /><p id=\"caption-attachment-2066302\" class=\"wp-caption-text\"><strong>Image Credits:</strong> Lightricks</p></div></p>\n<p>Users can then use Filtertune to edit photos with any of the custom filters discovered from across social media.</p>\n<p>It is interesting to see how much Filtertune leans on Instagram to drive discovery here. Even the &#8220;Discover&#8221; button in the app, when tapped, takes you directly to <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/explore/tags/filtertune/\">the #filtertune hashtag on Instagram,</a> instead of a dedicated section within its own app where users could find new filters to try.</p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"5LxK9M22Oi\"><p><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2020/07/28/facetune-maker-lightricks-brings-its-popular-selfie-retouching-features-to-video/\">Facetune maker Lightricks brings its popular selfie retouching features to video</a></p></blockquote>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts\" security=\"restricted\" title=\"&#8220;Facetune maker Lightricks brings its popular selfie retouching features to video&#8221; &#8212; TechCrunch\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/2020/07/28/facetune-maker-lightricks-brings-its-popular-selfie-retouching-features-to-video/embed/#?secret=5LxK9M22Oi\" data-secret=\"5LxK9M22Oi\" width=\"800\" height=\"450\" frameborder=\"0\" marginwidth=\"0\" marginheight=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"></iframe></div>\n<p>&#8220;Filtertune represents a natural evolution of our growing product experiences, and with it, Lightricks will continue fostering a culture of online community, sharing, and collaboration that is necessary for young artists, creators, and anyone who enjoys social media,” said Zeev Farbman, co-founder and CEO at Lightricks, in a statement about the new app&#8217;s launch.</p>\n<p>Farbman also noted that Lightricks&#8217; Facetune2 and Quickshot apps have seen a 30% increase and a 35% increase in users in 2020, respectively. The company also told TechCrunch that Ligthtricks, overall, has seen a 45% increase in monthly active users this year.</p>\n<p>The new app is a <a href=\"https://apps.apple.com/app/filtertune-filters-presets/id1511547935\">free download on iOS. </a></p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a 00:53:35","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 00:53:35","title":"Ubisoft’s subscription service comes to Stadia and Luna","link":"https://techcrunch.com/?p=2066324","description":"<p id=\"speakable-summary\"><a class=\"crunchbase-link\" href=\"https://crunchbase.com/organization/ubisoft\" target=\"_blank\" data-type=\"organization\" data-entity=\"ubisoft\">Ubisoft <span class=\"crunchbase-tooltip-indicator\"></span></a> <a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2019/06/10/ubisoft-is-launching-a-15-a-month-subscription-service-in-september/\">originally announced</a> its subscription service back in June. Today, the company is rebranding the service from UPlay+ to Ubisoft+. The service is also on its way to Amazon&#8217;s Luna and Google&#8217;s Stadia. <a class=\"crunchbase-link\" href=\"https://crunchbase.com/organization/ubisoft\" target=\"_blank\" data-type=\"organization\" data-entity=\"ubisoft\">Ubisoft <span class=\"crunchbase-tooltip-indicator\"></span></a> is betting on a multi-platform subscription, which means that you’ll be able to subscribe once and play Ubisoft+ games on PC, Amazon Luna and Stadia.</p>\n<p>Ubisoft+ is already available on PC. For $14.99 a month, you can download and play more than 100 games — the service includes both classics and newly released titles, such as games in the Splinter Cell and Prince of Persia franchises as well as the company’s upcoming releases. Assassin’s Creed Valhalla, Watch Dogs Legion and Immortals Fenyx Rising will be available in the Ubisoft+ library on their respective launch days.</p>\n<p>Ubisoft is trying to include premium editions of the games so that you don’t have to pay for game passes to access additional content. For instance, you can play the ultimate editions of Rainbow Six Siege, The Division 2, Assassin’s Creed Odyssey, etc.</p><div class=\"piano-inline-promo\"></div>\n<p>On November 10, you’ll be able to access Ubisoft+ games on <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Luna/\">Amazon Luna</a> is you’re beta testing Amazon’s cloud gaming service. And Google will also let you connect your Ubisoft+ account with Stadia by the end of the year. Interestingly, you don’t need to pay for Stadia Pro to access Ubisoft+ titles.</p>\n<p>Ubisoft is working on cross-platform progression, starting with upcoming titles. It’s a subscription focused on content, not platforms.</p>\n<p>As you can see, Microsoft and Sony don’t support Ubisoft+. It means that you won’t be able to subscribe and play on your Xbox or PlayStation. Console manufacturers take a cut on game purchases. That’s why negotiations between third-party game studios and console manufacturers are more complicated.</p>\n<p><div id=\"attachment_2066325\" style=\"width: 970px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><img aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-2066325\" loading=\"lazy\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Ubisoft_Rebranding.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"960\" height=\"540\" https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Ubisoft_Rebranding.jpg?resize=768,432 768w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Ubisoft_Rebranding.jpg?resize=680,383 680w, id=\"speakable-summary\"><a class=\"crunchbase-link\" href=\"https://crunchbase.com/organization/netflix\" target=\"_blank\" data-type=\"organization\" data-entity=\"netflix\">Netflix <span class=\"crunchbase-tooltip-indicator\"></span></a> announced this morning that it&#8217;s partnering with Ubisoft to adapt the game publisher&#8217;s &#8220;Assassin&#8217;s Creed&#8221; franchise into a live action series.</p>\n<p>The franchise jumps around in history, telling the story of a secret society of assassins with &#8220;genetic memory&#8221; and their centuries-long battle the knights templar. It has sold 155 million games worldwide and was also turned into a nearly incomprehensible 2016 film starring Michael Fassbender and Marion Cotillard, which <a href=\"https://www.boxofficemojo.com/release/rl4265772545/\">underperformed at the box office</a>.</p>\n<p>The companies say that they&#8217;re currently looking for a showrunner. Jason Altman and Danielle Kreinik of <a class=\"crunchbase-link\" href=\"https://crunchbase.com/organization/ubisoft\" target=\"_blank\" data-type=\"organization\" data-entity=\"ubisoft\">Ubisoft&#8217;s <span class=\"crunchbase-tooltip-indicator\"></span></a> film and television division will serve as executive producers. (In addition to working on adaptations of Ubisoft&#8217;s intellectual property, <a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2020/02/09/apple-mythic-quest/\">the publisher is also involved in the Apple TV+ industry comedy &#8220;Mythic Quest.&#8221;</a>)</p><div class=\"piano-inline-promo\"></div>\n<p>&#8220;We’re excited to partner with Ubisoft and bring to life the rich, multilayered storytelling that Assassin’s Creed is beloved for,” said Netflix&#8217;s vice president of original series Peter Friedlander in a statement. “From its breathtaking historical worlds and massive global appeal as one of the best selling video game franchises of all time, we are committed to carefully crafting epic and thrilling entertainment based on this distinct IP and provide a deeper dive for fans and our members around the world to enjoy.”</p>\n<p>It sounds like there could be follow-up shows as well, with the announcement saying that Netflix and Ubisoft will &#8220;tap into the iconic video game’s trove of dynamic stories with global mass appeal for adaptations of live action, animated, and anime series.&#8221;</p>\n<p>Netflix recently <a href=\"https://deadline.com/2020/08/resident-evil-tv-series-a-go-netflix-spoilers-plot-dual-timelines-andrew-dabb-ep-supernatural-1203024450/\">placed an eight-episode order for &#8220;Resident Evil,&#8221;</a> another video game franchise that was previously adapted for the big screen. And it also had a big hit with <a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2019/12/28/original-content-podcast-netflixs-witcher-shows-off-big-muscles-and-bigger-monsters/\">its adaptation of &#8220;The Witcher,&#8221;</a> which is based on a fantasy book series that was popularized via video games.</p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\"
